[name](repo): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=id) → description
- [Natural Language Dates](https://github.com/argenos/nldates-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=nldates-obsidian) → Create date-links based on natural language.
- [Hotkeys++](https://github.com/argenos/hotkeysplus-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=hotkeysplus-obsidian) → Additional hotkeys to do common things.
- [Git](https://github.com/Vinzent03/obsidian-git): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-git) → Integrate Git version control with automatic backup and other advanced features.
- [Paste URL into selection](https://github.com/denolehov/obsidian-url-into-selection): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=url-into-selection) → Paste URL "into" selected text.
- [Advanced Tables](https://github.com/tgrosinger/advanced-tables-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=table-editor-obsidian) → Improved table navigation, formatting, and manipulation.
- [Leader Hotkeys](https://github.com/tgrosinger/leader-hotkeys-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=leader-hotkeys-obsidian) → Add leader hotkey support to any command (like tmux or vim).
- [Recent Files](https://github.com/tgrosinger/recent-files-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=recent-files-obsidian) → Display a list of recently opened files.
- [Ledger](https://github.com/tgrosinger/ledger-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=ledger-obsidian) → Plain text accounting.
- [Note Refactor](https://github.com/lynchjames/note-refactor-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=note-refactor-obsidian) → Extract note content into new notes and split notes.
- [Calendar](https://github.com/liamcain/obsidian-calendar-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=calendar) → Simple calendar widget.
- [Text expand](https://github.com/mrjackphil/obsidian-text-expand): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=mrj-text-expand) → Search and paste/transclude links to found files.
- [Jump to link](https://github.com/mrjackphil/obsidian-jump-to-link): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=mrj-jump-to-link) → Quickly navigate between links, or jump to any word on the page using hotkeys.
- [Reading Time](https://github.com/avr/obsidian-reading-time): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-reading-time) → Add the current note's reading time to the status bar.
- [Todoist Sync](https://github.com/jamiebrynes7/obsidian-todoist-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=todoist-sync-plugin) → Materialize Todoist tasks within your notes.
- [Vimrc Support](https://github.com/esm7/obsidian-vimrc-support): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-vimrc-support) → Auto-load a startup file with Vim commands.
- [Shortcuts extender](https://github.com/ryjjin/Obsidian-shortcuts-extender): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=shortcuts-extender) → Use shortcuts for input special symbols without language switching.
- [Add links to current note](https://github.com/mrjackphil/obsidian-crosslink-between-notes): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=mrj-crosslink-between-notes) → A command to add a link to the current note at the bottom of selected notes.
- [Quick Switcher++](https://github.com/darlal/obsidian-switcher-plus): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=darlal-switcher-plus) → Enhanced Quick Switcher, search open panels, and symbols.
- [Day Planner](https://github.com/ivan-lednev/obsidian-day-planner): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-day-planner) → Day planning from a task list in a Markdown note with enhanced time block functionality.
- [Review](https://github.com/ryanjamurphy/review-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=review-obsidian) → Add a link to the current note to a daily note on a future date (or a past date, you time traveller).
- [Hider](https://github.com/kepano/obsidian-hider): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-hider) → Hide UI elements such as tooltips, status, titlebar and more.
- [Minimal Theme Settings](https://github.com/kepano/obsidian-minimal-settings): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-minimal-settings) → Control the colors and fonts in Minimal Theme.
- [Discord Rich Presence](https://github.com/lukeleppan/obsidian-discordrpc): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-discordrpc) → Update your Discord Status to show your friends what you are working on.
- [Templater](https://github.com/SilentVoid13/Templater): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=templater-obsidian) → Create and use templates.
- [Convert url to preview (iframe)](https://github.com/FHachez/obsidian-convert-url-to-iframe): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=convert-url-to-iframe) → Convert a URL (e.g. YouTube) into an iframe (preview).
- [Search++](https://github.com/nhaouari/searchpp): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=searchpp) → Insert text context search results in the active note.
- [Better Word Count](https://github.com/lukeleppan/better-word-count): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=better-word-count) → Count the words of selected text in the editor.
- [Workbench](https://github.com/ryanjamurphy/workbench-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=workbench-obsidian) → Keep a workbench of knowledge materials.
- [Latex Environments](https://github.com/raineszm/obsidian-latex-environments): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-latex-environments) → Quickly insert and change LaTeX environments within math environments.
- [RTL Support](https://github.com/esm7/obsidian-rtl): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-rtl) → Right-to-left (RTL) text direction support for languages like Arabic, Hebrew, and Farsi.
- [Markdown prettifier](https://github.com/cristianvasquez/obsidian-prettify): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=markdown-prettifier) → Fix and reformats ugly Markdown.
- [css snippets](https://github.com/jdbrice/obsidian-css-snippets): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=css-snippets) → Load and manage CSS snippets.
- [Link indexer](https://github.com/aviskase/obsidian-link-indexer): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-link-indexer) → Generate index notes with links based on various conditions.
- [macOS Keyboard Navigation](https://github.com/ryanjamurphy/macOS-keyboard-nav-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=macOS-keyboard-nav-obsidian) → Enable alt+↑ and alt+↓ keyboard navigation.
- [Extract Highlights](https://github.com/akaalias/extract-highlights-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=extract-highlights-plugin) → Extract all ==highlights== in a note into your clipboard.
- [Find orphaned files and broken links](https://github.com/Vinzent03/find-unlinked-files): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=find-unlinked-files) → Find files that are not linked anywhere and would otherwise be lost in your vault. In other words: files with no backlinks.
- [Wikilinks to MDLinks](https://github.com/agathauy/wikilinks-to-mdlinks-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=wikilinks-to-mdlinks-obsidian) → Convert wikilinks to Markdown links and vice versa.
- [Smart Random Note](https://github.com/erichalldev/obsidian-smart-random-note): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=smart-random-note) → Open random notes with greater control.
- [Tab Switcher](https://github.com/Vinzent03/tab-switcher): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=cycle-through-panes) → Switch your tabs with Ctrl + Tab in recently used order like in a browser.
- [ABC Music Notation](https://github.com/abcjs-music/obsidian-plugin-abcjs): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=music-code-blocks) → Render music sheets directly from code blocks using ABC music notation via abcjs.
- [Typewriter Scroll](https://github.com/deathau/cm-typewriter-scroll-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=cm-typewriter-scroll-obsidian) → Typewriter-style scrolling which keeps the view centered in the editor.
- [Youglish](https://github.com/nhaouari/obsidian-youglish-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-youglish-plugin) → Use YouTube to improve your pronunciation. YouGlish gives you fast, unbiased answers about how words is spoken by real people and in context.
- [Dangling links](https://github.com/graydon/obsidian-dangling-links): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-dangling-links) → Add a sidebar showing any dangling links in a vault. Dangling links are orphaned links that don't point to anything in the vault.
- [Dangerzone Writing](https://github.com/akaalias/dangerzone-writing-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=dangerzone-writing-plugin) → This plugin is dangerous! When you start it, you have to write without stopping for 100 seconds. If you stop, think and look around, after 3 seconds the plugin will DELETE what you've written in this note.
- [Maximise Active Pane](https://github.com/deathau/maximise-active-pane-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=maximise-active-pane-obsidian) → Fill the workspace with the active pane.
- [Julian Date](https://github.com/THeK3nger/obsidian-juliandate): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-juliandate) → Add a shortcut to insert the current Julian date for astronomical observations.
- [Emoji Toolbar](https://github.com/oliveryh/obsidian-emoji-toolbar): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-emoji-toolbar) → Quickly search for and insert emojis into your editor.
- [Fullscreen Focus Mode](https://github.com/Razumihin/obsidian-fullscreen-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-fullscreen-plugin) → Add a command to view a single document leaf in a fullscreen focus mode.
- [Footlinks](https://github.com/DahaWong/obsidian-footlinks): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=footlinks) → Extract URLs from main text to footer.
- [Mind Map](https://github.com/lynchjames/obsidian-mind-map): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-mind-map) → Display Markdown notes as mind maps using Markmap.
- [Flashcards](https://github.com/reuseman/flashcards-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=flashcards-obsidian) → Anki integration.
- [Completed Area](https://github.com/DahaWong/obsidian-completed-area): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=completed-area) → Move completed to-do items to a separate completed area.
- [Citations](https://github.com/hans/obsidian-citation-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-citation-plugin) → Automatically search and insert citations from a Zotero library.
- [Export to Anki](https://github.com/ObsidianToAnki/Obsidian_to_Anki): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-to-anki-plugin) → Anki integration designed for efficient bulk exporting. Previously known as Obsidian_to_Anki.
- [Rollover Daily Todos](https://github.com/lumoe/obsidian-rollover-daily-todos): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-rollover-daily-todos) → Rollover any unchecked checkboxes from your last daily note into today's note.
- [Automatically reveal active file](https://github.com/shichongrui/obsidian-reveal-active-file): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-reveal-active-file) → Automatically reveal the currently active file in the side navigation.
- [Export To TeX](https://github.com/raineszm/obsidian-export-to-tex): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-export-to-tex) → Export vault files in a format amenable to pasting into a TeX document.
- [Extended MathJax](https://github.com/wei2912/obsidian-latex): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-latex) → Enable additional MathJax packages and adds a global preamble for MathJax.
- [Apple Reminders](https://github.com/urishiraval/obsidian-apple-reminders-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-apple-reminders-plugin) → Import Apple Reminders.
- [Contextual Typography](https://github.com/mgmeyers/obsidian-contextual-typography): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-contextual-typography) → Add a data-tag-name attribute to all top-level divs in preview mode containing the child's tag name, allowing contextual typography styling.
- [Neo4j Graph View](https://github.com/HEmile/obsidian-neo4j-graph-view): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=neo4j-graph-view) → Advanced graph visualization and querying using Neo4j.
- [Snippets](https://github.com/cristianvasquez/obsidian-snippets-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=snippets) → Execute simple scripts/snippets. This plugin is experimental.
- [Temple](https://github.com/garyng/obsidian-temple): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-temple) → Templating powered by Nunjucks.
- [Relative Line Numbers](https://github.com/nadavspi/obsidian-relative-line-numbers): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-relative-line-numbers) → Enable relative line numbers in editor mode.
- [Charts](https://github.com/phibr0/obsidian-charts): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-charts) → Easily create interactive charts in your notes.
- [Discordian Theme](https://github.com/radekkozak/discordian-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=discordian-plugin) → Fine-grained control of Discordian Theme.
- [Autocomplete](https://github.com/yeboster/autocomplete-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-autocomplete-plugin) → Autocomplete text to increase your typing speed.
- [Completed Task Display](https://github.com/heliostatic/completed-task-display): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=completed-task-display) → Controls for displaying or hiding completed tasks.
- [PDF Highlights](https://github.com/akaalias/obsidian-extract-pdf-highlights): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-extract-pdf-highlights) → Extract highlights, underlines and annotations from your PDFs.
- [YouHaveBeenStaring](https://github.com/fxal/obsidian-youhavebeenstaring-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=youhavebeenstaring-plugin) → Add a status bar indicator showing how long your vault has been open.
- [Imgur](https://github.com/gavvvr/obsidian-imgur-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-imgur-plugin) → Upload images from your clipboard to imgur.com and embeds uploaded image to your note.
- [Checklist](https://github.com/delashum/obsidian-checklist-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-checklist-plugin) → Consolidate checklists across all files into a single view.
- [Search on Internet](https://github.com/HEmile/obsidian-search-on-internet): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=search-on-internet) → Add context menu items to search the internet based on the title of your note.
- [File path to URI](https://github.com/MichalBures/obsidian-file-path-to-uri): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-file-path-to-uri) → Convert file path to URI for easier use of links to local files outside of Obsidian.
- [Page Heading From Links](https://github.com/beet/page-headings-obsidian-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=page-heading-from-links) → Populate page headings from the file name.
- [Icons](https://github.com/visini/obsidian-icons-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-icons-plugin) → Add icons to your notes.
- [Folder Note](https://github.com/xpgo/obsidian-folder-note-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=folder-note-plugin) → Add description note to a folder.
- [Vantage - Advanced search builder](https://github.com/ryanjamurphy/vantage-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=vantage-obsidian) → Build advanced search queries.
- [Sort & Permute lines](https://github.com/Vinzent03/obsidian-sort-and-permute-lines): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-sort-and-permute-lines) → Sort and Permute lines in whole file or selection.
- [Min3ditorHotkeys](https://github.com/d-sauer/Obsidian-Min3ditorHotkeys-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-min3ditorhotkeys-plugin) → Additional editor hotkeys inspired by coding editors.
- [JSONifier](https://github.com/KjellConnelly/obsidian-jsonifier): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-jsonifier) → JSON.stringify() or JSON.parse() highlighted text and copy to clipboard.
- [Things Logbook](https://github.com/liamcain/obsidian-things-logbook): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=things-logbook) → Sync your Things logbook with your daily notes.
- [Hotkeys for Bookmarks](https://github.com/Vinzent03/obsidian-shortcuts-for-starred-files): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-shortcuts-for-starred-files) → Set an individual hotkey for the first 9 bookmarked files and open them just with your keyboard.
- [Filename Heading Sync](https://github.com/dvcrn/obsidian-filename-heading-sync): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-filename-heading-sync) → Keep the filename with the first heading of a file in sync.
- [Orthography](https://github.com/denisoed/obsidian-orthography): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-orthography) → Check & fix orthography errors in text.
- [Obsidian Query Language](https://github.com/jplattel/obsidian-query-language): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-query-language) → Query notes and represent data.
- [Markdown Formatting Assistant](https://github.com/Reocin/obsidian-markdown-formatting-assistant-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-markdown-formatting-assistant-plugin) → A formatting sidebar for Markdown and a command line interface to facilitate a faster workflow.
- [Journey](https://github.com/akaalias/obsidian-journey-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-journey-plugin) → Discover the story between your notes.
- [Tag Wrangler](https://github.com/pjeby/tag-wrangler): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=tag-wrangler) → Rename, merge, toggle, and search tags from the tag pane.
- [Better PDF](https://github.com/MSzturc/obsidian-better-pdf-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=better-pdf-plugin) → Insert, scale, rotate and cut-out PDF pages into your notes.
- [Dataview](https://github.com/blacksmithgu/obsidian-dataview): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=dataview) → Advanced queries over your vault for the data-obsessed.
- [Periodic Notes](https://github.com/liamcain/obsidian-periodic-notes): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=periodic-notes) → Create/manage your daily, weekly, and monthly notes.
- [Show Current File Path](https://github.com/ravimashru/obsidian-show-file-path): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-show-file-path) → Show the full path of the currently open file in the status bar.
- [Various Complements](https://github.com/tadashi-aikawa/obsidian-various-complements-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=various-complements) → Complete words similar to auto-completion in an IDE.
- [Note Folder Autorename](https://github.com/pjeby/note-folder-autorename): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=note-folder-autorename) → Turn notes into folders and automatically move/rename their folders when they move or are renamed.
- [Daily Activity](https://github.com/trydalch/obsidian-daily-activity): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=daily-activity) → Output a list of the files changed/created today in the active file.
- [Daily Stats](https://github.com/dhruvik7/obsidian-daily-stats): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-daily-stats) → Track your daily word count.
- [Custom window title](https://github.com/jplattel/open-note-to-window-title): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=open-note-to-window-title) → Show the current open note in the window title.
- [Meld Encrypt](https://github.com/meld-cp/obsidian-encrypt): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=meld-encrypt) → Hide secrets in your notes.
- [Vault Statistics](https://github.com/bkyle/obsidian-vault-statistics-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-vault-statistics-plugin) → Status bar item with vault statistics such as number of notes, files, attachments, and links.
- [TODO | Text-based GTD](https://github.com/larslockefeer/obsidian-plugin-todo): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-plugin-todo) → Collect all outstanding TODOs from your vault and presents them in lists Today, Scheduled, Inbox and Someday/Maybe.
- [Hotkeys for specific files](https://github.com/Vinzent03/obsidian-hotkeys-for-specific-files): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-hotkeys-for-specific-files) → Add commands for specific files and open them with a hotkey.
- [CSV Editor](https://github.com/deathau/csv-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=csv-obsidian) → Edit CSV files.
- [Table of Contents](https://github.com/hipstersmoothie/obsidian-plugin-toc): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-plugin-toc) → Create a table of contents for a note.
- [Mochi Cards Exporter](https://github.com/kalibetre/mochi-cards-exporter): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=mochi-cards-exporter) → Export Markdown notes to Mochi cards.
- [Prettier Format](https://github.com/hipstersmoothie/obsidian-plugin-prettier): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-plugin-prettier) → Opinionated formatting for your notes.
- [Furigana](https://github.com/uonr/obsidian-furigana): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-furigana) → Display furigana using ruby syntax.
- [Vault Changelog](https://github.com/philoserf/obsidian-vault-changelog): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-vault-changelog) → Maintain a changelog of recently edited notes.
- [Chesser](https://github.com/SilentVoid13/Chesser): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=chesser-obsidian) → A chess game viewer/editor.
- [Chessboard Viewer](https://github.com/THeK3nger/obsidian-chessboard): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-chessboard) → Render chess positions diagrams in note preview.
- [Footnote Shortcut](https://github.com/MichaBrugger/obsidian-footnotes): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-footnotes) → Makes creating footnotes more fun!
- [NoteTweet](https://github.com/chhoumann/notetweet_obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=notetweet) → Post to Twitter.
- [Code block from selection](https://github.com/dy-sh/obsidian-code-block-from-selection): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=code-block-from-selection) → Turn the selected text into a code block.
- [Format Hotkeys](https://github.com/anstosa/format-hotkeys-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=format-hotkeys-obsidian) → Google Docs style formatting hotkeys.
- [Leaflet](https://github.com/javalent/obsidian-leaflet): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-leaflet-plugin) → Interactive maps inside your notes.
- [Remember cursor position](https://github.com/dy-sh/obsidian-remember-cursor-position): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=remember-cursor-position) → Remember cursor and scroll position for each note.
- [Pane Relief](https://github.com/pjeby/pane-relief): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=pane-relief) → Per-pane history, hotkeys for pane movement + navigation, and more.
- [DEVONlink](https://github.com/ryanjamurphy/DEVONlink-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=DEVONlink-obsidian) → Open or reveal the current note in DEVONthink.
- [Hotkey Helper](https://github.com/pjeby/hotkey-helper): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=hotkey-helper) → Easily see and access any plugin's settings or hotkey assignments (and conflicts) from the Community Plugins tab.
- [Text Snippets](https://github.com/ArianaKhit/text-snippets-obsidian): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=text-snippets-obsidian) → Snippets for faster typing. Replace text templates, create your own, and expand text shortcuts.
- [Consistent attachments and links](https://github.com/dy-sh/obsidian-consistent-attachments-and-links): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=consistent-attachments-and-links) → Move note attachments and update links automatically.
- [PlantUML](https://github.com/joethei/obsidian-plantuml): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-plantuml) → Generate PlantUML diagrams.
- [Open cards in imdone.](https://github.com/imdone/imdone-obsidian-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=imdone-obsidian-plugin) → Open cards in imdone kanban from their source in Obsidian.
- [Unique attachments](https://github.com/dy-sh/obsidian-unique-attachments): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=unique-attachments) → Rename attachments, making their names unique (based on hashing of file content).
- [Dice Roller](https://github.com/javalent/dice-roller): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-dice-roller) → Add a little randomness to your notes!
- [LanguageTool Integration](https://github.com/Clemens-E/obsidian-languagetool-plugin): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-languagetool-plugin) → advanced spell/grammar checks with the help of language-tool.
- [Outliner](https://github.com/vslinko/obsidian-outliner): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-outliner) → Work with your lists like in Workflowy or Roam Research.
- [Extract url content](https://github.com/trashhalo/obsidian-extract-url): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=extract-url) → Extract URL converting content into Markdown.
- [Find and replace in selection](https://github.com/dy-sh/obsidian-find-and-replace-in-selection): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=find-and-replace-in-selection) → Find what you are looking for in the selected text and replace it with the specified text.
- [Buttons](https://github.com/shabegom/buttons): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=buttons) → Create Buttons in your notes to run commands, open links, and insert templates.
- [Admonition](https://github.com/javalent/admonitions): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-admonition) → Admonition block-styled content.
- [Tracker](https://github.com/pyrochlore/obsidian-tracker): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-tracker) → Track occurrences and numbers in your notes.
- [Hotkeys for templates](https://github.com/Vinzent03/obsidian-hotkeys-for-templates): [install](obsidian://show-plugin?id=obsidian-hotkeys-for-templates) → Add commands to insert specific templates with a hotkey.
